<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {
        var
                ui5ico = '.ui5ico',
                $ui5ico = $(ui5ico),
                ui5icoStyle = [];

        $ui5ico.each(function () {
            var
                    ui5icoDataName = 'data-ui5ico',
                    ui5icoContent = $(this).attr(ui5icoDataName).toLowerCase().trim(),
                    ui5icoDataSelector = ui5ico + '[' + ui5icoDataName + '=' + ui5icoContent + ']';

            if (ui5icoContent.startsWith('x')) {
                var ui5icoContent = ui5icoContent.replace('x', '');
            }

            var
                    ui5icoContent = '"\\' + ui5icoContent + '"',
                    ui5icoCSSRule = ui5icoDataSelector + ':before{content:' + ui5icoContent + '!important;}';

            if (ui5icoStyle.includes(ui5icoCSSRule) == false) {
                ui5icoStyle.push(ui5icoCSSRule);
            }
        });

        var
                ui5icoStyle = ui5icoStyle.join(''),
                ui5icoStyle = '<style type="text/css">' + ui5icoStyle + '</style>';

        $('head').append(ui5icoStyle);
    });
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
    function myFunction() {
        var topbar = document.getElementsByClassName("nav-pills");
        var langLink = document.getElementsByClassName("languageselector");
        var langList = document.getElementsByClassName("headerdropdown");
        var profile = document.getElementsByClassName("profileWidget").children;
        var list1 = document.createElement("li");
        var list2 = document.createElement("li");

        list1.classList.add("custom-menu-item1");
        list2.classList.add("custom-menu-item2");
        list1.appendChild(langLink);
        list1.appendChild(langList);
        list2.appendChild(profile);

        topbar.appendChild(list1);
        topbar.appendChild(list2);
    }
    //window.onload = myFunction;
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $.fn.isInViewport = function() {
        var top = $('.customPlugin.customPlugin-69087bbf1b184c0a').outerHeight(true);
        return $(document).scrollTop() >= top;
    };

    $(window).on('load resize scroll', function() {
        $('#header').each(function() {
            if ($(this).isInViewport()) {
                if (!$('#header').find('.search.displayDTM').length) {
                    $('.search.displayDTM').clone().appendTo('#header');
                }
            } else if (!$(this).isInViewport()){
                $('#header').find('.search.displayDTM').remove();
            }
        });
    });
</script>

                .mapcontainer {

            <script type="text/javascript">

                //<![CDATA[
                var getHashValue = function (key) {
                    var matches = location.hash.match(new RegExp(key + '=([^&]*)'));
                    return matches ? matches[1] : null;
                };

                var buildIframeUrl = function () {
                    var zoom = "",
                            center = "",
                            keyword = "",
                            regionCode = "";

                    if (getHashValue('zoom')) {
                        zoom = getHashValue('zoom');
                    } else {
                        zoom = '2';
                    }

                    if (getHashValue('center')) {
                        center = getHashValue('center');
                    } else {
                        center = '25,5';
                    }

                    if (getHashValue('keyword')) {
                        keyword = getHashValue('keyword');
                    }

                    if (getHashValue('regionCode')) {
                        regionCode = getHashValue('regionCode');
                    } else {
                        regionCode = 'US';
                    }

                    var url = "https://";
                    url += "rmk-map-12.jobs2web.com/map/";
                    url += "?esid=0ghFSsXoty969Bgrw%2BmvyQ%3D%3D&locale=en_US&uselcl=false&watercolor=%23f4f4f4";
                    url += "&jobdomain=jobs.sap.com";
                    url += "&maplbljob=Job";
                    url += "&maplbljobs=jobs";
                    url += "&mapbtnsearchjobs=Search+jobs";
                    url += "&centerpoint=" + center + "&mapzoom=" + zoom + "&keyword=" + keyword;
                    url += "&regionCode=" + regionCode;
                    url += "&mapbrand=";
                    url += '&limittobrand=true'

                    return url;
                }

                //]]>
            </script>
                    <div class="map-hidden-content">
                        <h2>Screen readers cannot read the following searchable map.</h2>
                        <a href="/search/">Follow this link to reach our Job Search page to search for available jobs in a more accessible format.</a>
                    </div>
                            
                            <div class="mapcontainer">
                                <script type="text/javascript">
                                    //<![CDATA[

                                    // we need to pass along just the URL before the #, if it exists
                                    var href = 'http\x3A\x2F\x2Fjobs.sap.com\x2F';
                                    href = href.split("#")[0];

                                    var mapSrc = buildIframeUrl() + '&parentURL=' + encodeURIComponent(href) ;

                                    // name being set to Date.now() is to bust some weird caching issues
                                    document.write('<iframe id="iframe" title="Google job map" src="' + mapSrc + '" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" ></iframe>');

                                    // hack to force browser to not cache iframe results, even though URL may be different
                                    var _iframe = document.getElementById('iframe');
                                    _iframe.contentWindow.location.href = _iframe.src;

                                    //]]>
                                </script>
                            </div>
    </div>

    function deleteFooter() {
        var footerRowTop = document.querySelector("#footerRowTop");
        footerRowTop.remove();
        var footerRowBottom = document.querySelector("#footerRowBottom");
        footerRowBottom.remove();
        var footerColumnsShell = document.querySelector("#footerColumnsShell");
        footerColumnsShell.remove();
        var headersubmenu = document.querySelector(".lower.headersubmenu");
        headersubmenu.remove();
    }
    window.onload = deleteFooter;
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    function myFunction() {
        var topbar = document.querySelector(".nav-pills").lastChild;
        var langLink = document.querySelector(".languageselector");
        var langList = document.querySelector(".headerdropdown");
        var profile = document.querySelector(".profileWidget > a");
        var list1 = document.createElement("li");
        var list2 = document.createElement("li");

        list1.classList.add("custom-menu-item1");
        list2.classList.add("custom-menu-item2");
        list1.appendChild(langLink);
        list1.appendChild(langList);
        list2.appendChild(profile);

        topbar.after(list1);
        topbar.after(list2);

        var subMenu = document.querySelector(".lower.headersubmenu");
        subMenu.remove();
    }
    
    //window.onload = myFunction;

            <script type="text/javascript">
            //<![CDATA[
                if (Cookies && !Cookies.get('rmk12')) {
                    $('.ukCookiePolicy').show();

                    $('#cookie-close').click(function () {
                        closeBanner();
                    });

                    $('#cookie-acknowledge').click(function () {
                        closeBanner(true);
                    });

                    /**
                     * Closes the cookie banner, optionally dropping a cookie to keep the banner from reappearing.
                     * @param {boolean=} bDropCookie - If true, a cookie will be dropped to prevent the banner from
                     *     being shown again.
                     */
                    function closeBanner(bDropCookie) {
                        if (bDropCookie) {
                            Cookies.set('rmk12', 1, {
                                expires: (function () {
                                    var i = new Date;
                                    i.setFullYear(i.getFullYear() + 30);
                                    return i;
                                }())
                            });
                        }

                        $('div.ukCookiePolicy').remove();

                        /* When the banner is removed, the fixed header may need to be resized. If there is no fixed
                        header, this event goes unhandled. Please see header.xhtml. */
                        $(document).trigger('resizeFixedHeader');

                        $("#diversion").focus();
                    }
                }
            //]]>
            </script>
